init_pop_distrib = {
	set_global_variable = { name = pop_weight_total value = 0 }
	set_global_variable = { name = pop_total_mult value = $pop$ }
	change_global_variable = { name = pop_total_mult divide = 1000 }
	
	every_province = {
		limit = {
			geographical_region = $region$
		}
		change_global_variable = { name = pop_weight_total add = var:pop_weight }
		set_variable = { name = pop_total value = var:pop_weight }
		change_variable = { name = pop_total multiply = global_var:pop_total_mult }
	}
	
	every_province = {
		limit = {
			geographical_region = $region$
		}
		change_variable = { name = pop_total divide = global_var:pop_weight_total }
		change_variable = { name = pop_total multiply = 1000 }
		change_variable = { name = pop_total add = 1 }
	}
	
	remove_global_variable = pop_weight_total
	remove_global_variable = pop_total_mult
}
